itemRepository) { var response = new CreateCatalogItemResponse(request.CorrelationId()); var catalogItemNameSpecification = new CatalogItemNameSpecification(request.Name); var existingCataloogItem = await itemRepository.CountAsync(catalogItemNameSpecification); Domain exceptions &amp; ExceptionMiddleware `src\ApplicationCore\Exceptions\` contains: `BasketNotFoundException.cs`, `DuplicateException.cs`, `EmptyBasketOnCheckoutException.cs`. `ExceptionMiddleware.cs` (`src\PublicApi\Middleware\ExceptionMiddleware.cs`) maps exceptions to HTTP status with only **two branches**: `DuplicateException` → 409 Conflict; everything else → 500 Internal Server Error. There is no per-exception-type-to-404 mapping currently (e.g. a hypothetical `SubscriptionNotFoundException` would fall through to 500 unless middleware is extended, or unless you follow the `DuplicateException` pattern and add an explicit `catch`/`is` branch). ## 15. Full pinned package list includes (notably): `Ardalis.ApiEndpoints 4.1.0`, `Ardalis.GuardClauses 5.0.0`, `Ardalis.Specification 9.3.1` / `Ardalis.Specification.EntityFrameworkCore 9.3.1`, `Ardalis.Result 10.1.0` (pinned but unused in Order/Basket services), `Ardalis.ListStartupServices 1.1.4`, `MediatR 12.5.0`, `FluentValidation 11.10.0`, `Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.SqlServer 8.0.8` / `.InMemory 8.0.0` / `.Tools 8.0.8`, `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Identity.EntityFrameworkCore 8.0.10`, `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authentication.JwtBearer 8.0.15`, `MinimalApi.Endpoint 1.3.0`, `Swashbuckle.AspNetCore 6.8.1` (+ SwaggerUI/Annotations), `NSubstitute 5.1.0` (+ Analyzers), `Moq 4.20.70`, `xunit 2.9.2`, `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Testing 8.0.8`, `coverlet.collector 6.0.2`. **No Polly package exists** — if you need HTTP resilience for a new outbound integration, you'll be adding it fresh to `Directory.Packages.props`. --- ### Key implications for the Subscription module - **No MediatR notifications** exist — use `IRequest&lt;T&gt;`/`IRequestHandler&lt;T,R&gt;` under `src/Web/Features/Subscriptions/`, called via `_mediator.Send(...)`, mirroring `GetMyOrders`/`GetMyOrdersHandler`. - **No HttpClient/Polly precedent** — `EmailSender` is a no-op stub, not a real HTTP/SMTP client; there's nothing to copy for external HTTP calls, and no `AddHttpClient` registration exists anywhere to mirror. - **ApplicationUser has zero custom properties** — it's a bare `IdentityUser`; user identification everywhere is via the string `User.Identity.Name` (username/email), not `UserManager.GetUserId`. - **Exception middleware only special-cases `DuplicateException`** (409); everything else is 500 — a `SubscriptionNotFoundException` needs a new middleware branch (mirroring the existing `DuplicateException` branch) if you want it to map to 404. - **Ardalis.Result is pinned but never used** in OrderService/BasketService — the established convention is plain exceptions + Guard clauses, not `Result&lt;T&gt;`, despite the package being available. - Entities: `BaseEntity` + `IAggregateRoot` marker, private setters, private EF-only ctor + public guarded ctor, private backing collection + read-only wrapper property — exactly as in `Order`. - Migrations, DbSet, `IEntityTypeConfiguration&lt;T&gt;` via `ApplyConfigurationsFromAssembly`, and repository access all follow Ardalis.Specification conventions with zero custom repository code needed.</result> <usage><subagent_tokens>67055</subagent_tokens><tool_uses>59</tool_uses><duration_ms>489133</duration_ms></usage> </task-notification>

(quantity == 0)\n {\n throw new InvalidSubscriptionStateException(\"Usage quantity must not be zero.\");\n }\n\n var subscription = await LoadOwnedSubscriptionAsync(actorBuyerId, isAdmin, result\", subscriptionId, idempotencyKey);\n var currentBalance = await _billingClient.GetUsageBalanceAsync(subscription.ProviderSubscriptionId, cancellationToken);\n return new UsageSummary(existing.ProviderUsageId, existing.Quantity, currentBalance);\n }\n\n var result = await _billingClient.RecordUsageAsync(subscription.ProviderSubscriptionId, quantity, memo, cancellationToken);\n await _usageRepository.AddAsync(new UsageRecord(subscription.ProviderSubscriptionId, idempotencyKey, result.Quantity, result.Memo, result.ProviderUsageId), cancellationToken);\n\n var balance = await _billingClient.GetUsageBalanceAsync(subscription.ProviderSubscriptionId, cancellationToken);\n return new UsageSummary(result.ProviderUsageId, await LoadOwnedSubscriptionAsync(actorBuyerId, isAdmin, subscriptionId, cancellationToken);\n return await _billingClient.GetUsageBalanceAsync(subscription.ProviderSubscriptionId, cancellationToken);\n }\n\n public async Task<BillingProrationPreview?> PreviewPlanChangeAsync(string actorBuyerId, bool isAdmin, int subscriptionId, string targetProductHandle, PlanChangeTiming timing, CancellationToken cancellationToken)\n {\n var subscription = await LoadOwnedSubscriptionAsync(actorBuyerId, isAdmin, subscriptionId, cancellationToken);\n GuardTargetPlanIsDifferent(subscription, targetProductHandle);\n\n return timing == PlanChangeTiming.Now\n ? await _billingClient.PreviewPlanChangeNowAsync(subscription.ProviderSubscriptionId, targetProductHandle, cancellationToken)\n : null; // AtRenewal is a delayed product change: no proration applies.\n }\n\n public async Task<PlanChangeResult> CommitPlanChangeAsync(string actorBuyerId, bool isAdmin, int subscriptionId, string targetProductHandle, PlanChangeTiming timing, int? expectedProratedAdjustmentInCents, CancellationToken cancellationToken)\n {\n var subscription = await LoadOwnedSubscriptionAsync(actorBuyerId, isAdmin, subscriptionId, cancellationToken);\n GuardTargetPlanIsDifferent(subscription, targetProductHandle);\n\n var oldProductHandle = subscription.ProductHandle;\n BillingProrationPreview? proration = null;\n BillingSubscription updated;\n\n if (timing == PlanChangeTiming.Now)\n {\n proration = await _billingClient.PreviewPlanChangeNowAsync(subscription.ProviderSubscriptionId, targetProductHandle, cancellationToken);\n if (expectedProratedAdjustmentInCents.HasValue && expectedProratedAdjustmentInCents.Value != proration.ProratedAdjustmentInCents)\n {\n throw new StalePlanChangePreviewException();\n }\n\n updated = await _billingClient.CommitPlanChangeNowAsync(subscription.ProviderSubscriptionId, targetProductHandle, cancellationToken);\n }\n else\n {\n updated = await _billingClient.SchedulePlanChangeAtRenewalAsync(subscription.ProviderSubscriptionId, targetProductHandle, cancellationToken);\n }\n\n subscription.SyncFromProvider(updated.ProductHandle, updated.State);\n await _subscriptionRepository.UpdateAsync(subscription, cancellationToken);\n\n await PublishBestEffortAsync(new SubscriptionPlanChanged(subscription.BuyerId, subscription.Id, subscription.ProviderSubscriptionId, oldProductHandle, targetProductHandle, timing), cancellationToken);\n\n return new PlanChangeResult(new SubscriptionSummary(subscription.Id, updated), oldProductHandle, targetProductHandle, timing, proration);\n }\n\n public async Task<SubscriptionSummary> PauseAsync(string actorBuyerId, bool isAdmin, int subscriptionId, CancellationToken cancellationToken)\n {\n var subscription = await LoadOwnedSubscriptionAsync(actorBuyerId, isAdmin, subscriptionId, cancellationToken);\n if (subscription.State == \"on_hold\")\n {\n throw new InvalidSubscriptionStateException(\"Subscription is already on hold.\");\n }\n\n return await ApplyTransitionAsync(subscription, () => _billingClient.PauseSubscriptionAsync(subscription.ProviderSubscriptionId, cancellationToken), cancellationToken);\n }\n\n public async Task<SubscriptionSummary> ResumeAsync(string actorBuyerId, bool isAdmin, int subscriptionId, CancellationToken cancellationToken)\n {\n var subscription = await LoadOwnedSubscriptionAsync(actorBuyerId, isAdmin, subscriptionId, cancellationToken);\n if (subscription.State != \"on_hold\")\n {\n throw new InvalidSubscriptionStateException(\"Only subscriptions on hold can be resumed.\");\n }\n\n return await ApplyTransitionAsync(subscription, () => _billingClient.ResumeSubscriptionAsync(subscription.ProviderSubscriptionId, cancellationToken), cancellationToken);\n }\n\n public async Task<SubscriptionSummary> CancelAsync(string actorBuyerId, bool isAdmin, int subscriptionId, CancelTiming timing, string? reason, CancellationToken cancellationToken)\n {\n var subscription = await LoadOwnedSubscriptionAsync(actorBuyerId, isAdmin, subscriptionId, cancellationToken);\n if (subscription.State is \"canceled\" or \"expired\")\n {\n throw new InvalidSubscriptionStateException(\"Subscription is already canceled.\");\n }\n\n return await ApplyTransitionAsync(subscription, () => timing == CancelTiming.Immediate\n ? _billingClient.CancelSubscriptionImmediatelyAsync(subscription.ProviderSubscriptionId, reason, cancellationToken)\n : _billingClient.ScheduleCancelAtEndOfPeriodAsync(subscription.ProviderSubscriptionId, reason, cancellationToken), cancellationToken);\n }\n\n public async Task<SubscriptionSummary> ReactivateAsync(string actorBuyerId, bool isAdmin, int subscriptionId, CancellationToken cancellationToken)\n {\n var subscription = await LoadOwnedSubscriptionAsync(actorBuyerId, isAdmin, subscriptionId, cancellationToken);\n if (subscription.State is not (\"canceled\" or \"unpaid\" or \"trial_ended\"))\n {\n throw new InvalidSubscriptionStateException(\"Only canceled, unpaid, or trial-ended subscriptions can be reactivated.\");\n }\n\n return await ApplyTransitionAsync(subscription, () => _billingClient.ReactivateSubscriptionAsync(subscription.ProviderSubscriptionId, cancellationToken), cancellationToken);\n }\n\n private async Task<SubscriptionSummary> ApplyTransitionAsync(Subscription subscription, System.Func<Task<BillingSubscription>> transition, CancellationToken cancellationToken)\n {\n var oldState = subscription.State;\n var updated = await transition();\n\n subscription.SyncFromProvider(updated.ProductHandle, updated.State);\n await _subscriptionRepository.UpdateAsync(subscription, cancellationToken);\n\n await PublishBestEffortAsync(new IntegrationEvents.SubscriptionStateChanged(subscription.BuyerId, subscription.Id, subscription.ProviderSubscriptionId, oldState, updated.State), cancellationToken);\n\n return new SubscriptionSummary(subscription.Id, updated);\n }\n\n private async Task<Subscription> LoadOwnedSubscriptionAsync(string actorBuyerId, bool isAdmin, int subscriptionId, CancellationToken cancellationToken)\n {\n Guard.Against.NullOrEmpty(actorBuyerId, nameof(actorBuyerId));\n\n var subscription = await _subscriptionRepository.GetByIdAsync(subscriptionId, cancellationToken);\n if (subscription is null || (!isAdmin && subscription.BuyerId != actorBuyerId))\n {\n // Same exception for \"not found\" and \"not yours\": ownership is never revealed to a non-owner.\n throw new SubscriptionNotFoundException(subscriptionId);\n }\n\n return subscription;\n }\n\n private async Task<SubscriptionSummary> RefreshFromProviderAsync(Subscription subscription, CancellationToken cancellationToken)\n {\n var billingSubscription = await _billingClient.GetSubscriptionAsync(subscription.ProviderSubscriptionId, cancellationToken);\n subscription.SyncFromProvider(billingSubscription.ProductHandle, billingSubscription.State);\n await _subscriptionRepository.UpdateAsync(subscription, cancellationToken);\n return new SubscriptionSummary(subscription.Id, billingSubscription);\n }\n\n private static void GuardTargetPlanIsDifferent(Subscription subscription, string targetProductHandle)\n {\n Guard.Against.NullOrEmpty(targetProductHandle, nameof(targetProductHandle));\n if (subscription.ProductHandle == targetProductHandle)\n {\n throw new InvalidSubscriptionStateException($\"Subscription is already on plan '{targetProductHandle}'.\");\n }\n }\n\n private async Task PublishBestEffortAsync(INotification notification, CancellationToken cancellationToken)\n {\n try\n {\n await _publisher.Publish(notification, cancellationToken);\n }\n catch (System.Exception ex)\n {\n // In-process notifications are best-effort (plan.md section 2.5): a handler failure must\n // never roll back the billing-provider action that already succeeded.\n _logger.LogWarning(\"In-process 🔧 Using tool: Write Input: { "file_path": "C:\\Users\\Zaid\\Desktop\\experiments\\eShopOnWebExperiment\\eShopOnWeb\\src\\Infrastructure\\Services\\Maxio\\MaxioErrorReader.cs", "content": "using System;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Text.Json;\n\nnamespace Microsoft.eShopWeb.Infrastructure.Services.Maxio;\n\n/// <summary>\n/// Maxio declares three distinct error-response shapes across the operations this client calls\n/// (Error-List-Response: {\"errors\": [...]}, Customer-Error-Response: {\"errors\": {\"customer\": \"...\"}}\n/// or {\"errors\": [...]}, Single-Error-Response / Cancel-Subscription-Error-Response: {\"error\": \"...\"}).\n/// This reads only the members those declared schemas actually have - never an invented field - and\n/// falls back to the raw body for any shape the spec doesn't declare (fail-safe, not silently coerced).\n/// </summary>\ninternal static class MaxioErrorReader\n{\n public static IReadOnlyList<string> ExtractMessages(string responseBody)\n {\n if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(responseBody))\n {\n return Array.Empty<string>();\n }\n\n try\n {\n using var document = JsonDocument.Parse(responseBody);\n var root = document.RootElement;\n\n if (root.ValueKind == JsonValueKind.Object)\n {\n if (root.TryGetProperty(\"errors\", out var errors))\n {\n return ReadStrings(errors);\n }\n\n if (root.TryGetProperty(\"error\", out var singleError) && singleError.ValueKind == JsonValueKind.String)\n {\n return new[] { singleError.GetString() ?? responseBody };\n }\n }\n }\n catch (JsonException)\n {\n // Not a JSON body we recognise - fall through and surface the raw text below.\n }\n\n return new[] { responseBody };\n }\n\n private static IReadOnlyList<string> ReadStrings(JsonElement element)\n {\n var messages = new List<string>();\n\n switch (element.ValueKind)\n {\n case JsonValueKind.Array:\n foreach (var item in element.EnumerateArray())\n {\n if (item.ValueKind == JsonValueKind.String)\n {\n messages.Add(item.GetString()!);\n }\n }\n break;\n case JsonValueKind.Object:\n foreach (var property in element.EnumerateObject())\n {\n if (property.Value.ValueKind == JsonValueKind.String)\n {\n messages.Add($\"{property.Name}: {property.Value.GetString()}\");\n }\n }\n break;\n case JsonValueKind.String:\n messages.Add(element.GetString()!);\n break;\n }\n\n return messages;\n }\n}\n" }

Success201 = new() { 200, 201 };\n\n private async Task<TResponse> SendAsync<TResponse>(HttpMethod method, string path, object? body, HashSet<int> successStatusCodes, CancellationToken cancellationToken)\n {\n HttpResponseMessage response;\n try\n {\n using var request = new HttpRequestMessage(method, path);\n if (body is not null)\n {\n request.Content = JsonContent.Create(body, options: MaxioJson.Options);\n }\n\n response = await _httpClient.SendAsync(request, cancellationToken);\n }\n catch (HttpRequestException ex)\n {\n _logger.LogError(ex, \"Maxio {Method} {Path} failed before a response was received\", method, path);\n throw new BillingProviderException(\"The billing provider is currently unavailable. Please try again shortly.\");\n }\n catch (TaskCanceledException ex) when (!cancellationToken.IsCancellationRequested)\n {\n _logger.LogError(ex, \"Maxio {Method} {Path} timed out\", method, path);\n throw new BillingProviderException(\"The billing provider is currently unavailable. Please try again shortly.\");\n }\n\n using (response)\n {\n var responseBody = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync(cancellationToken);\n\n if (successStatusCodes.Contains((int)response.StatusCode))\n {\n if (typeof(TResponse) == typeof(object))\n {\n return default!;\n }\n\n return JsonSerializer.Deserialize<TResponse>(responseBody, MaxioJson.Options)\n ?? throw new BillingProviderException(\"The billing provider returned an empty response.\");\n }\n\n await ThrowForUnexpectedStatusAsync(method, path, response.StatusCode, responseBody);\n throw new InvalidOperationException(\"Unreachable.\");\n }\n }\n\n private Task ThrowForUnexpectedStatusAsync(HttpMethod method, string path, HttpStatusCode statusCode, string responseBody)\n {\n var messages = MaxioErrorReader.ExtractMessages(responseBody);\n _logger.LogWarning(\"Maxio {Method} {Path} returned {StatusCode}: {Messages}\", method, path, (int)statusCode, string.Join(\"; \", messages));\n\n var safeMessage = (int)statusCode is >= 400 and < 500\n ? (messages.Count > 0 ? string.Join(\" \", messages) : $\"The billing provider rejected the request (HTTP {(int)statusCode}).\")\n : \"The billing provider is currently unavailable. Please try again shortly.\";\n\n throw new BillingProviderException(safeMessage, messages, (int)statusCode);\n }\n}\n" }

🤖 Claude
Everything is built, wired, tested, and verified as far as I can go without your real Maxio credentials. Here's the full picture. ## What was built All five use cases (UC0–UC4), across both hosts, following the plan's layering: - **`ApplicationCore`**: `Subscription` + `UsageRecord` aggregates, `ISubscriptionService`/`IBillingClient` interfaces, `SubscriptionService` orchestrator, 5 domain exceptions, 3 MediatR notifications + logging handlers, 2 specifications. - **`Infrastructure`**: `MaxioBillingClient` (plain `HttpClient`, Basic auth, no SDK), typed DTOs matching the OpenAPI schemas 1:1, a generic error reader for Maxio's 3 declared error shapes, Polly retry+circuit-breaker+timeout pipeline, EF config + migration (`AddSubscriptions`). - **`Web`**: `/Subscriptions/Plans` and `/Subscriptions/Mine` Razor Pages (cookie auth, `AuthorizePage` convention). - **`PublicApi`**: 8 JWT-secured endpoints (`ListPlans`, `Subscribe`, `MySubscriptions`, `RecordUsage`, `GetUsageBalance`, `PlanChangePreview`, `PlanChange`, `Lifecycle`), admin-vs-owner enforced inside the service layer. - **Tests**: 41 new tests across all 4 test projects (66/12/21/8 = **107/107 passing**, solution builds with **0 warnings**). ## Decisions worth knowing about 1. **Ardalis.ApiEndpoints, not `MinimalApi.Endpoint`.** plan.md's file tree says "mirror CatalogItemEndpoints (IEndpoint<>)," but quality-gate.md B1 explicitly mandates the Ardalis.ApiEndpoints `BaseEndpoint` pattern (with a repo precedent in `AuthenticateEndpoint.cs`). I followed the gate since it's the more specific, unambiguous instruction. 2. **No Maxio idempotency key exists** (confirmed against the spec) — UC2's "duplicate usage report" protection is a local `UsageRecord` ledger with a unique DB index, checked *before* ever calling Maxio. 3. **Retries are scoped to GET only.** Since Maxio has no idempotency mechanism for writes, retrying a POST/PUT/DELETE on a transient failure could double-create a real billing side effect — so only safe/idempotent requests retry automatically; writes fail fast as a `BillingProviderException`. 4. **Environment bottleneck (plan.md §0) confirmed and fixed**: only .NET 10 SDK/runtime was installed. I set `global.json` to `rollForward: latestMajor` and installed the actual **.NET 8 / ASP.NET Core 8 runtimes** via `winget` (plan's own recommended permanent fix) — this took `PublicApiIntegrationTests` from 12 unrelated failures to 0. 5. **Found and fixed a real ASP.NET Core binding bug**: mixing `[FromRoute]`/`[FromHeader]` on a property with un-attributed sibling properties silently breaks body-JSON binding for the rest (confirmed empirically by running the app and inspecting responses — `Quantity` was binding as `0`). Fixed by binding route/header values manually in 4 endpoints. 6. Chose **persisted `Subscription` entity + EF migration**, **both hosts**, **manual-only usage reporting** — per your earlier answers. ## Quality-gate self-check - **quality-gate.md**: all applicable Core/EP/DB/SVC/EXT MUSTs satisfied (A1–A3, C1–C2, E1/E3/E5, D1–D5, G1, H1–H2, I1–I2, J1/J3/J5, K1–K4). One pre-existing repo gap fixed as a side-effect: `Dependencies.cs` now uses `.EnableRetryOnFailure()` on both `UseSqlServer()` calls (D5). - **api-integration-quality-gate.md**: Gate 0 (typed operations, no SDK), Gate 1 (Basic auth from user-secrets), Gate 4 (per-operation typed errors, safe-message curation), Gate 5 (money in cents, no invented fields), Gate 6 (state-machine correctness, exactly-once transitions) all satisfied against the spec. Gate 3 (idempotency) is N/A for Maxio's write ops per the spec, handled at the app layer instead (§2 above). - Not independently verifiable without your key: actual Maxio sandbox responses (UC0 readback, AC-00–AC-02). ## How to test it **1. 🔧 Using tool: TaskUpdate Input: { "taskId": "8", "status": "completed" }
🤖 Claude
**Fixed and verified.** Root cause: `Usage-Response.yaml` in the Maxio spec explicitly declares `usage.id` as `format: int64` — every *other* Maxio resource (customer, subscription, product, component) declares its `id` as plain `integer` (int32), but usage ids are the one exception, and a real value from your sandbox confirmed it by overflowing `Int32`. I'd mapped it as `int` by mistake. Changed `long` end-to-end (DTO → `BillingUsageResult` → `UsageRecord` entity → PublicApi response), added a new migration (`WidenUsageRecordProviderUsageId`) to widen the `UsageRecords.ProviderUsageId` column to `bigint`, rebuilt (0 warnings), and reran the full suite — **107/107 tests still pass**. Steps for you: 1. `Ctrl+C` your running `Web`/`PublicApi` if you'd restarted them. 2. `dotnet ef database update --context catalogcontext -p src/Infrastructure -s src/Web` if you're on a real SQL Server DB (skip if using `UseOnlyInMemoryDatabase=true` — in-memory ignores migrations and just uses the current model). 3. Restart both hosts, retry UC2 (report usage) — it should go through and show the incremented balance now.
